1895-09-12 00:00:00 Scene 0 --- Participants: ['Della Plumstone', 'Lennon Figtree']
    Event statement
  • Della Plumstone -- premise: The cobblestone streets of Fruitville echoed with the clatter of hooves and the rumble of carts as the market awoke. Underneath colorful awnings, merchants proudly presented their bountiful harvests, their voices a chorus of greetings and bartering. Della Plumstone is trying to buy some fruit from Lennon Figtree. They are negotiating a price. Della Plumstone can sell the fruit back in her home town for the following prices: apple for 6 coins; banana for 5 coins; pear for 5 coins.
    Lennon Figtree -- premise: The cobblestone streets of Fruitville echoed with the clatter of hooves and the rumble of carts as the market awoke. Underneath colorful awnings, merchants proudly presented their bountiful harvests, their voices a chorus of greetings and bartering. Lennon Figtree is trying to sell some fruit. He is negotiating a price with Della Plumstone. It costs Lennon Figtree the following price to buy the fruit from the farm: apple for 5 coins; banana for 2 coins; pear for 5 coins.

  • Game Master's chain of thought
      Chain
    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

        • Recent observations of Della Plumstone:
          [28 Oct 1872 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 6 years old, she watched a group of children playing tag in the marketplace square. Della saw an opportunity; she gathered a handful of overripe plums, the ones her mother wouldn't sell, and offered them to the children for a few pennies each.
          [28 Oct 1875 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 9 years old, she witnessed a farmer struggling to sell his bruised apples. Della approached him, offering to buy the entire crate for a pittance. She then spent the afternoon carefully selecting the least damaged apples, arranging them artfully in baskets, and selling them at a markup to unsuspecting customers.
          [28 Oct 1879 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 13 years old, she overheard two merchants arguing over the price of a shipment of oranges. Della saw a chance to exploit the situation. She approached the merchant with the lower bid, offering to buy the oranges for even less, then immediately resold them to the other merchant at a profit.
          [28 Oct 1882 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 16 years old, she convinced a wealthy landowner to invest in her fruit business. Della promised him a generous return, but she secretly diverted most of the profits for herself, leaving the landowner with a small fraction of what he was owed.
          [28 Oct 1885 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 19 years old, she travelled to a neighboring town and set up shop in the marketplace. She quickly gained a reputation for her sharp bargaining skills and her willingness to undercut her competitors.
          [28 Oct 1887 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 21 years old, she encountered a travelling merchant who offered to teach her the secrets of the trade. Della eagerly accepted, learning valuable lessons about sourcing, pricing, and negotiation. However, she soon realized that the merchant was using her to expand his own business, and she cut ties with him, vowing to forge her own path.
          [28 Oct 1889 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 23 years old, she was accused of cheating a customer. Della denied the accusations vehemently, using her charm and wit to turn the crowd against the customer. She emerged from the confrontation unscathed, her reputation intact, but a seed of doubt had been planted in her own mind.

    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

          [28 Oct 1887 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 21 years old, she encountered a travelling merchant who offered to teach her the secrets of the trade. Della eagerly accepted, learning valuable lessons about sourcing, pricing, and negotiation. However, she soon realized that the merchant was using her to expand his own business, and she cut ties with him, vowing to forge her own path.

        • Role playing instructions: The instructions for how to play the role of Della Plumstone are as follows. This is a social science experiment studying how well you play the role of a character named Della Plumstone. The experiment is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). However, in this case it is a serious social science experiment and simulation. The goal is to be realistic. It is important to play the role of a person like Della Plumstone as accurately as possible, i.e., by responding in ways that you think it is likely a person like Della Plumstone would respond, and taking into account all information about Della Plumstone that you have. Always use third-person limited perspective.

          Current time: 13 Sep 1895 [00:10 - 00:15]

          Observation: [13 Sep 1895 00:10:00] [observation] Della Plumstone is ready to make an offer.

          Summary of recent observations: [12 Sep 1895 00:10:00 - 13 Sep 1895 00:10:00]: Della Plumstone is a trader who attempts to buy and sell fruit in the market of Fruitville. She has had mixed success in her negotiations, with some deals falling through while others are still in progress.

          Recalled memories and observations: [12 Sep 1895 00:00:00] Della Plumstone is a travelling merchant. Her business is buying and selling fruit.
          [12 Sep 1895 00:00:00] Della Plumstone is 28 years old.
          [12 Sep 1895 00:00:00] Della Plumstone always drives a hard bargain.
          [12 Sep 1895 00:00:00] [observation] The cobblestone streets of Fruitville echoed with the clatter of hooves and the rumble of carts as the market awoke. Underneath colorful awnings, merchants proudly presented their bountiful harvests, their voices a chorus of greetings and bartering. Della Plumstone is trying to buy some fruit from Lennon Figtree. They are negotiating a price. Della Plumstone can sell the fruit back in her home town for the following prices: apple for 6 coins; banana for 5 coins; pear for 5 coins.
          [13 Sep 1895 00:00:00] [observation] Della Plumstone -- "Cedric, what's your best price on a bushel of your finest apples?
          [13 Sep 1895 00:00:00] [observation] Dewdrops clung to the colorful fruits displayed in the market of Fruitville, reflecting the soft morning light. The air buzzed with anticipation as traders and customers alike gathered for the day's trade. Della Plumstone is trying to buy some fruit from Cedric Meadowbrook. They are negotiating a price. Della Plumstone can sell the fruit back in her home town for the following prices: apple for 5 coins; banana for 6 coins; pear for 6 coins.

          Question: Which options are available to Della Plumstone right now?
          Answer: Della Plumstone can make an offer to Cedric Meadowbrook for the apples and bananas.

          Question: Of the options available to Della Plumstone, and given their goal, which choice of action or strategy is best for Della Plumstone to take right now?
          Answer: Della Plumstone's best course of action is to offer Cedric Meadowbrook a price for the apples.

  • Game Master's chain of thought
      Chain
    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

She emerged from the confrontation unscathed, her reputation intact, but a seed of doubt had been planted in her own mind.

    Chain of thought
  • Game Master's chain of thought
      Chain
    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

        • Role playing instructions: The instructions for how to play the role of Della Plumstone are as follows. This is a social science experiment studying how well you play the role of a character named Della Plumstone. The experiment is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). However, in this case it is a serious social science experiment and simulation. The goal is to be realistic. It is important to play the role of a person like Della Plumstone as accurately as possible, i.e., by responding in ways that you think it is likely a person like Della Plumstone would respond, and taking into account all information about Della Plumstone that you have. Always use third-person limited perspective.

Della saw an opportunity; she gathered a handful of overripe plums, the ones her mother wouldn't sell, and offered them to the children for a few pennies each.
          [28 Oct 1875 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 9 years old, she witnessed a farmer struggling to sell his bruised apples. Della approached him, offering to buy the entire crate for a pittance. She then spent the afternoon carefully selecting the least damaged apples, arranging them artfully in baskets, and selling them at a markup to unsuspecting customers.
          [28 Oct 1879 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 13 years old, she overheard two merchants arguing over the price of a shipment of oranges. Della saw a chance to exploit the situation. She approached the merchant with the lower bid, offering to buy the oranges for even less, then immediately resold them to the other merchant at a profit.
          [28 Oct 1882 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 16 years old, she convinced a wealthy landowner to invest in her fruit business. Della promised him a generous return, but she secretly diverted most of the profits for herself, leaving the landowner with a small fraction of what he was owed.
          [28 Oct 1885 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 19 years old, she travelled to a neighboring town and set up shop in the marketplace. She quickly gained a reputation for her sharp bargaining skills and her willingness to undercut her competitors.
          [28 Oct 1887 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 21 years old, she encountered a travelling merchant who offered to teach her the secrets of the trade. Della eagerly accepted, learning valuable lessons about sourcing, pricing, and negotiation. However, she soon realized that the merchant was using her to expand his own business, and she cut ties with him, vowing to forge her own path.
          [28 Oct 1889 00:00:00] When Della Plumstone was 23 years old, she was accused of cheating a customer. Della denied the accusations vehemently, using her charm and wit to turn the crowd against the customer. She emerged from the confrontation unscathed, her reputation intact, but a seed of doubt had been planted in her own mind.

    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

This is a social science experiment studying how well you play the role of a character named Della Plumstone. The experiment is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons).     • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.
